posted:Posted May 7, 2024
msg:The hotel is quite new, with a luxurious appearance. Parking is very convenient. You can park in the basement. It is newly opened and free. The dark stone floor and red wall of the lobby form a strong visual contrast. There is a modern Chinese style. The lobby has a rest area and free tea, which is quite humane. There are four elevators to the guest room floors. You can swipe your card to take the elevator. You can only swipe the floor you live on. The carpet on the floor of the public corridor is matched with dark wood veneer and red paint on the wall. It is a continuation of the lobby style. The style is also very good. The door closer is heavy and a bit difficult to push. In addition, the sound insulation of the door is average. The room is quite spacious, especially the width is very large. The interior is mainly decorated with wood veneer wallpaper and hard packing. At present, there is still a bit of the smell of a new house. Fortunately, the windows can be opened for ventilation. Electric curtains. The wall of the TV is made of wood veneer background, and the size of the TV is slightly small. There is a small garden table that can be used for multiple purposes. If there is no desk, use it. There is a recliner with footrests by the window. It is quite relieving to lie on it and prop up your feet when you are tired from traveling. It would be better if there is a massage chair. The twin beds don't seem very wide. I wonder if they can be combined into a large bed? I haven't tried it. The bathroom sink and the sleeping area are separated by a glass sliding door. This design is quite good. The washing area is particularly large. There is a refrigerator under the countertop. There are snacks left by the previous tenants. It seems that this place is often forgotten when cleaning. There are also snack packaging boxes left at the end of the curtain. These two places are probably more likely to be missed. The toilet and shower are separate rooms. They look very high-end. The downside is that there is no brand on the toilet and shower. The toilet is very ordinary and cold when sitting on it. The glaze is not smooth enough. The shower has a top spray, which looks very high-end at first glance, but the top spray leaks even if it is fully opened to the handheld shower. The shower gel and shampoo have a good fragrance. There are a lot of people on the 6th floor for breakfast. You need to queue up for breakfast on holidays. You need to wait for a seat if you come down at 9 o'clock. Fortunately, the hotel food is updated very quickly.

msg:I have been using Ctrip for 8 years, and this is the first time I want to write about my grievances! I am also a frequent hotel stayer, and I usually give good reviews and make careful comments! When I left Qianjiangwan New Century Grand Hotel yesterday, my mood was at its lowest point! 
I booked New Century online on April 22, because the experience of staying at New Century in Pingyang County, Zhejiang was very good. I searched for New Century Hotel as soon as I arrived in Hangzhou. I checked in at the front desk, and the front desk helped me upgrade from a twin room to a deluxe twin bed. I was very grateful! As soon as I arrived in the room, the corridor smelled like a new house decoration. I comforted myself that the newly renovated hotel was like this. As a result, as soon as I arrived in the room, I opened the window of the room for ventilation, and a few meters downstairs was the rumbling noise of the air conditioner and pipes. Due to the fatigue of the journey, I did not come downstairs to change rooms immediately, because we also had a lot of luggage and were too sleepy! 
After waking up the next day, I went downstairs to continue my stay and reported the situation. A manager at the front desk immediately reported my situation to the general manager of the front desk (a lady). The manager gave me a room card for the 20th floor. Due to the bed type, we could only live on the side facing the pipes. The noise could not be solved. We could only move to a higher floor from the 10th floor. I also went to the 20th floor to see if the noise was louder on the top floor? The room also smelled bad, but the view and lighting were good. I thought about it and decided not to change the room because the noise was only at night.
During the few days of stay, the following problems occurred:
1. The wifi could not be connected on the second day, so the engineering depar**ent came to fix it
2. The takeaway robot arrived at the door, but the landline could not be reached, so the robot went down by itself. The takeaway arrived at the hotel for 20 minutes, but we did not eat it. The hotel arranged for the engineering depar**ent to repair it, and the takeaway was cold by the time we ate it
3. Because the landline could not reach the front desk phone, I used my mobile phone to call the front desk of Qianjiangwan Kaiyuan Hotel on Ctrip, explaining that the robot delivery landline did not ring, and by the way, I said that I would extend my stay today and come down to pay later in the afternoon. After the landline was repaired, the front desk called me and I also explained that I wanted to extend my stay! This is the problem! When I went to the first floor to pay for the extension at 4 pm, I was told that my room was booked! ! ! ! ! The front desk staff also said, look, these guests have booked rooms, but there are no rooms available. What was in my heart? ? ? Later, no matter how I negotiated, they said there were no rooms. Here I really want to say that as a chain brand, Kaiyuan has not conducted systematic professional training! Guests who have already checked in and are not sure whether they will stay the next day should call to ask if they will stay the next day. After confirming with the guest, the room will be booked out! The attitude of the front desk is really bad. They are all "busy". I feel sad, embarrassed, caught off guard, and disrespected. I have repeatedly said that I want to stay longer, and they have booked our room. Are they driving us away? In this case, is it the professionalism that a chain brand hotel should have without a word of apology or attitude? Why didn't we leave in this situation? It's because we have a lot of luggage, and we are tired from the journey and the clothes are not dry, so we are too lazy to change hotels. Later, I didn't want to stay longer, so I said you swipe the room card for me and I will go to pack my luggage.
What was very speechless was that when I went downstairs to the front desk to check out, the front desk said: I won't charge you any extra room fees. I was really speechless at the time. The front desk didn't say a word of apology, and said that they didn't charge me for the extended room fee. From their expressions, they all looked indifferent. In the end, I watched me move five pieces of luggage from the front desk alone, and no one helped.
We are not saying that Qianjiangwan Hotel is useless.
The hotel has a wide variety of breakfasts, rich and fresh, and it is worth staying in
The engineering depar**ent's technicians came to the door quickly and were very polite. Thank you very much
